function adv_hyp_brand(pc,ul,bg,lg,nam,hole){
    if (document.body.className.indexOf('header_fixed')==-1)document.body.className=document.body.className+' header_brand header_brand_fix header_brand_'+lg;
    else document.body.className=document.body.className+' header_brand_fix header_brand_'+lg;
    document.body.style.backgroundColor=bg;
    document.body.style.backgroundImage='none';
    if(document.getElementById("adv_wallpaper"))document.getElementById("adv_wallpaper").style.display = 'block';
    if(document.getElementById("adv_wallpaper2")){
        var wp=document.getElementById("adv_wallpaper2");
        wp.href=ul;
        wp.setAttribute("target", "_blank");
        wp.style.height="2500px";
    }
    var d=document.getElementById('hd_brandheader');
    d.style.backgroundImage="url("+pc+")";
    d.href=ul;
    d.target="_blank";
    _brandheader=true;
    document.getElementById('hp_hook-970x90-1').style.display='none';
    //brandheader viewability
    window.scrollTo(0, 0);
}
function adv_hyp_brand2(pc,ul,bg,lg,nam,hole){

    else document.body.className=document.body.className+' header_brand_fix header_brand_'+lg;
    if(document.getElementById("adv_wallpaper"))document.getElementById("adv_wallpaper").style.display = 'block';

        var wp=document.getElementById("adv_wallpaper2");
        wp.href=ul;
        wp.setAttribute("target", "_blank");

    d.target="_blank";
    _brandheader=true;
    document.getElementById('hp_hook-970x90-1').style.display='none';
    //brandheader viewability
    window.scrollTo(0, 0);
}

function iol_advBrandheaderDisplay(prms){ // pc,ul,bg,lg,nam,hole
		var ul = prms.landing;
		var pc = prms.small_image;
		var bg = prms.bgcolor;
		var lg = prms.logo;
		if(typeof prms.large_image != undefined) {
			if (prms.large_image) {
				var wdth = document.getElementById("hp_container").offsetWidth;
				if(wdth >= 1190) pc = prms.large_image;
			}
		}
    if (document.body.className.indexOf('header_fixed')==-1)document.body.className=document.body.className+' header_brand header_brand_fix header_brand_'+lg;
    else document.body.className=document.body.className+' header_brand_fix header_brand_'+lg;
    document.body.style.backgroundColor=bg;
    document.body.style.backgroundImage='none';
    if(document.getElementById("adv_wallpaper"))document.getElementById("adv_wallpaper").style.display = 'block';
    if(document.getElementById("adv_wallpaper2")){
        var wp=document.getElementById("adv_wallpaper2");
        wp.href=ul;
        wp.setAttribute("target", "_blank");
        wp.style.height="2500px";
    }
    var d=document.getElementById('hd_brandheader');
    d.style.backgroundImage="url("+pc+")";
    d.href=ul;
    d.target="_blank";
    _brandheader=true;
    document.getElementById('hp_hook-970x90-1').style.display='none';
	
	try{
	  var styleTag = $('<style id="adv_brand"></style>'),
					styleRules = '.bh_t1 {background:' + bg + ' url(' + pc + ') no-repeat 50% 0;}#bh_area-click{position:absolute; top:0; left:0; width:100%; height:2500px;}#bh_link{cursor:pointer; display:block; width:100%; height:100%;}',
					divClick = $('<div id="bh_area-click"></div>'),
					anchorTag = $('<a id="bh_link" href="' + ul + '" target="_blank"></a>');
				$('body').prepend(divClick.html(anchorTag));
				$('head').append(styleTag.html(styleRules));
	}catch(ex){}
	
    //brandheader viewability
    window.scrollTo(0, 0);
}

function getParameterByName(name) {
	var res = new RegExp('[\?&]'+name.replace(/\[/g, '\\\[').replace(/\]/g, '\\\]')+'(?:=([^&#]*))?(?:[&#]|$)').exec(window.location.search);
	return res ? (res[1] ? decodeURIComponent(res[1].replace(/\+/g, ' ')) : '') : null;
}

                admputop.appendTo(hook300x250_3);
                admpumiddle.appendTo(hook300x250_6);
                admpufoot.appendTo(hook300x250_8);

                _precDimension = 970;
            }
            if (mainW >= 730 && mainW < 970) {
                // console.log('posizione tablet portrait e desktop');
                promo1.appendTo(hookLocal300x250_1);

                admputop.appendTo(hook300x250_2);
                admpumiddle.appendTo(hook300x250_5);
                admpufoot.appendTo(hook300x250_7);

                _precDimension = 730;
            }
            if (mainW < 730) {
                // console.log('mobile e phonblet tablet 7' portrait');

                admputop.appendTo(hook300x250_1);
                admpumiddle.appendTo(hook300x250_4);
                admpufoot.appendTo(hook300x250_8);

                _precDimension = 560;
            }
            if (mainW < 560) {
                // console.log('mobile < 560');
                promo1.appendTo(hookLocal300x250_1);

                _precDimension = 300;
            }
        },
        resolvePrecDimension: function() {
            if (mainW >= 970) {
                _precDimension = 970;
            }
            if (mainW >= 730 && mainW < 970) {
                _precDimension = 730;
            }
            if (mainW < 730) {
                _precDimension = 560;
            }
            if (mainW < 560) {
                _precDimension = 300;
            }
        },
        loadAdv: function() {
            googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                googletag.pubads().refresh();
            });
        },
        reLoadAdv: function() {
            this.loadAdv();
        }
    };
})();
//e: gestione posizioni adv

function advLocalVenduto(){
    var main = $('#hp_main'), mainW = main.width();
    if ($('#promo1').length > 0 && (mainW >= 560 && mainW < 730)) {
        $('#promo1').parent('.hp_local-sponsor').hide();
        $('#promo1').parent('.hp_local-sponsor').siblings('.hp_local-board').show();
    } else {
        $('#promo1').parent('.hp_local-sponsor').show();
        $('#promo1').parent('.hp_local-sponsor').siblings('.hp_local-board').hide();
    }
}

        s.async = "async";

        $("body").append(s);
    }

	biReturnUrl: function(objEl){

		var _biReturnUrl = objEl.attr('href');
		if(!_biReturnUrl) {
			return '';
		}
		var _biReturnUrlGo = _biReturnUrl;

		if(jQuery.isFunction(objEl.attr('onclick')))
		{
			objEl.attr('data-bi-urlClick', objEl.attr('onclick'));
			if (objEl.attr('action'))
				objEl.attr('data-bi-form', objEl.attr('id'));
			else
				objEl.attr('data-bi-form', null);

			objEl.attr('onclick', null);
			_biReturnUrlGo="";
		}







		if(objEl.attr('href').indexOf("javascript:")!=-1)
			_biReturnUrl="";

		objEl.attr('data-bi-anchor-url', _biReturnUrl);
		objEl.attr('data-bi-urlGo', _biReturnUrlGo);

		return _biReturnUrl;
	},

	removeParam: function(key, sourceURL) {
	    var rtn = sourceURL.split("?")[0],
	        param,
	        params_arr = [],
	        queryString = (sourceURL.indexOf("?") !== -1) ? sourceURL.split("?")[1] : "";
	    if (queryString !== "") {
	        params_arr = queryString.split("%3F");
	        for (var i = params_arr.length - 1; i >= 0; i -= 1) {
	            param = params_arr[i].split("%3D")[0];
	            if (param === key) {
	                params_arr.splice(i, 1);
	            }
	        }
	        rtn = rtn + "?" + params_arr.join("%3F");
	    }
	    return rtn;
	},

	biTrack:function (objBiToTrack){
		var vBiParamMacroArea="", vBiParamArea="", vBiParamSubArea="", vDataBiDomain="";
		var _vFunction = objBiToTrack.getAttribute('data-bi-preFnc');

		if (_vFunction){
			eval(_vFunction)(objBiToTrack);
		}

		var vDataBiCanale=objBiToTrack.getAttribute('data-bi-canale');
		var vDataBiUrl=objBiToTrack.getAttribute('data-bi-url');
		if (objBiToTrack.getAttribute('data-bi-url') == null){vDataBiUrl=objBiToTrack.getAttribute('data-bi-urlgo');}
		if (vDataBiUrl){
			try{
				vDataBiUrl = this.removeParam("rndPrx",vDataBiUrl);
				vDataBiUrl = this.removeParam("pnc",vDataBiUrl);
			}catch(ex){
				if(this.debug) {
					console.log(ex);
				}
			}

			try{
				var _vArrDataBiDomain = vDataBiUrl.split("/");
				if (objBiToTrack.getAttribute('href')){
					_vArrDataBiDomain = objBiToTrack.getAttribute('href').split("/");
				}

				var _vDataBiDomain = _vArrDataBiDomain[2];
				var _vArrDataBiDomainTmp = _vDataBiDomain.split("?");
				vDataBiDomain = _vArrDataBiDomainTmp[0];
			}catch(ex){
				if(this.debug) {
					console.log(ex);
				}
			}

			try{
				if (!vDataBiCanale){
					vDataBiCanale = this.remappingChannelFromUrl(vDataBiUrl);
					if (!vDataBiCanale){vDataBiCanale=vDataBiDomain;}
				}
			}catch(ex){
				if(this.debug) {
					console.log(ex);
				}
			}
		}

		var vDataBiId=objBiToTrack.getAttribute('data-bi-id');
		var vDataBiParam=objBiToTrack.getAttribute('data-bi-param');

		var vArrDataBiParam = vDataBiParam.split("|");

		var vDataBiResolution= this.biGetResolutionIolEvent();
		try{vBiParamMacroArea= vArrDataBiParam[0];}catch(ex){}
		try{vBiParamArea= vArrDataBiParam[1];}catch(ex){}
		try{vBiParamSubArea= vArrDataBiParam[2];}catch(ex){}



		if (this.debug){
			alert("BI param: " + vArrDataBiParam + "\n\nCanale: " + vDataBiCanale +  "\nUrl: " + vDataBiUrl);
		}

		try{
			var vTypeBiEvnt=objBiToTrack.getAttribute('data-bi-typeEvnt');
			if (vTypeBiEvnt){
				if ((vTypeBiEvnt=="iolmpck")||(vTypeBiEvnt=="iolck")){
					var _dataBiResolution = vDataBiResolution;
					if (_dataBiResolution == "0-559"){_dataBiResolution="559";}
					this.biClickIolEvent(objBiToTrack, vBiParamMacroArea, vBiParamArea, vBiParamSubArea, vDataBiCanale, _dataBiResolution, vDataBiUrl, vDataBiDomain, _ABTestingTrack);
				}
			}
		}catch(ex){
			if(this.debug) {
				console.log(ex);
			}
		}

		if (this.enableTrackComscore){
			Libero.click(objBiToTrack, {labels: {wa_cksrv_par_a: 'virgilio', wa_cksrv_par_b: lBI.biContainer, wa_cksrv_par_c: vBiParamMacroArea, wa_cksrv_par_d: vBiParamArea, wa_cksrv_par_e: vDataBiCanale, wa_cksrv_par_f: vBiParamSubArea,  wa_cksrv_resolution: vDataBiResolution, wa_cksrv_to: vDataBiUrl, wa_cksrv_domain_to: vDataBiDomain, wa_test_ab: _ABTestingTrack}});
		}
		return false;

	},

	biAriannaSearch : function (objBiToTrack, url, empty_url, vDataBiParam, vDataBiCanale, q, encode, target) {
		encode = encode == undefined ? 1 : encode;
		target = target == undefined ? null : target;

		var vArrDataBiParam = vDataBiParam.split("|");
		var vBiParamMacroArea="", vBiParamArea="", vBiParamSubArea="";
		try{vBiParamMacroArea= vArrDataBiParam[0];}catch(ex){}
		try{vBiParamArea= vArrDataBiParam[1];}catch(ex){}
		try{vBiParamSubArea= vArrDataBiParam[2];}catch(ex){}

		var vDataBiResolution=0;
		try{
			vDataBiResolution = $('#hp_main').width();
			if (vDataBiResolution < 560){
				vDataBiResolution = "0-559";
			}
		}catch(ex){
			if(this.debug) {
				console.log(ex);
			}
		}

		var vDataBiUrl = empty_url;

		// empty query
		if ( q.match(/^\s*$/) ) {
			if ( typeof(empty_url) != 'undefined' ) {
				//ckSrv(empty_url,cksrv_a,cksrv_b,cksrv_c,target);
				if(this.enableTrackComscore){
					Libero.click(objBiToTrack, {labels: {wa_cksrv_par_a: 'virgilio', wa_cksrv_par_b: lBI.biContainer, wa_cksrv_par_c: vBiParamMacroArea, wa_cksrv_par_d: vBiParamArea, wa_cksrv_par_e: vDataBiCanale, wa_cksrv_par_f: vBiParamSubArea, wa_cksrv_resolution: vDataBiResolution, wa_cksrv_to: vDataBiUrl, wa_test_ab: _ABTestingTrack}});
				}
				return false;
			}
			else
				return false;
		}
		else {
			//vDataBiUrl = url + ( encode ? encodeURIComponent(q) : q );
			vDataBiUrl = url;
			if(this.enableTrackComscore){
				Libero.click(objBiToTrack, {labels: {wa_cksrv_par_a: 'virgilio', wa_cksrv_par_b: lBI.biContainer, wa_cksrv_par_c: vBiParamMacroArea, wa_cksrv_par_d: vBiParamArea, wa_cksrv_par_e: vDataBiCanale, wa_cksrv_par_f: vBiParamSubArea, wa_cksrv_resolution: vDataBiResolution, wa_cksrv_to: vDataBiUrl, wa_test_ab: _ABTestingTrack}});
			}
			return false;
		}
	},


	biGetResolutionIolEvent : function(){
		var vDataBiResolution=0;
		try{
			vDataBiResolution = $('#hp_main').width();
			if (vDataBiResolution < 560){
				vDataBiResolution = "0-559";
			}
		}catch(ex){
			if(this.debug) {
				console.log(ex);
			}
		}
		return vDataBiResolution;
	},

	biClickIolEvent : function(objBiToTrack, vBiParamMacroArea, vBiParamArea, vBiParamSubArea, vDataBiCanale, vDataBiResolution, vDataBiUrl, vDataBiDomain, _ABTestingTrack){
		try {
			var _strilloId = "";
			var _profileCategory="";
			var _mapPosition = 0;

			var _trCanale = this.biIolTrCanale(vDataBiCanale, objBiToTrack.getAttribute('data-bi-url'));

			if (_trCanale){
				if (_trCanale.indexOf("undefined")== -1) {
						var _strilloId = this.biIolTrIdDetail(_trCanale, objBiToTrack.getAttribute('data-bi-id'));
				}
			}

			_profileCategory = this.biIolGetRtProfileCategory();
			_mapPosition = this.biIolPositionMap(objBiToTrack);

			IOL.EVNT.evMngr.sendEvents(IOL.EVNT.evMngr.getEventUrls("ck", {
					"domain"  : "wwwtest.virgilio.it",
					"pag_id" : "hp",
					"ref_host" : IOL.EVNT.evMngr.getHostFromUrl(document.referrer),
					"ref_path" : IOL.EVNT.evMngr.getPathFromUrl(document.referrer),
					"box_ctr_id" : _strilloId,
					"doc_type" : 9,
					"page" : "hp",
					"area" : vBiParamMacroArea,
					"box" : vBiParamArea,
					"link_type" : vBiParamSubArea,
					"cat1" : vDataBiCanale,
					"cat2" : vDataBiUrl,
					"cat3" : _ABTestingTrack,
					"dest_id" : _strilloId,
					"breakpoint" : vDataBiResolution,
					"mappa" : _mapPosition
			}), function() { /*console.log('evento click inviato');*/ } );
		}catch(ex){console.log(ex);}
	},

	biIolTrIdDetail: function (_trCanale, _tmpId){
		var _strID="";
		if (_tmpId){
			if (_tmpId.indexOf("_")!==-1){
				return _tmpId;
			}
			_strID=_tmpId;	
		}
		return _trCanale + "_" + _strID;
	},
	biIolTrCanale: function (_tmpCanale, _tmpurl){
		var _canale=_tmpCanale;
		var _url="";
		if(!_tmpurl){
			return _tmpCanale;
		}

		try{
			_tmpurl = _tmpurl.trim();
			var re = /^(?:https?:\/\/)?(?:[^@\n]+@)?(?:www\.)?([^:\/\n]+)/igm;
	        var m = re.exec(_tmpurl);
			_url = m[1].replace(".it","").replace(".org","").replace(".com","").replace(".virgilio","").replace(".libero","").replace(".vitv","").replace(".","");
			_url = _url.split('?')[0];

			if (_canale.indexOf("community")!=-1){
				_url = "community";
			}

		}catch(ex){
			if(this.debug) {
				console.log(ex);
			}
		}

		try{
			if (_url){
				_url = _url.replace(".it","").replace(".org","").replace(".com","").replace(".virgilio","").replace(".vitv","").replace("http://","").replace(".","");
			}

			if (_tmpCanale.indexOf("mediaset")!=-1){
				_canale = "mediaset";
			}
			//return _canale + "_" + _url;
			return _canale.toLowerCase();
		}catch(ex){return _tmpCanale + "_" + _url;}
	},

	biIolGetRtProfileCategory: function(){
		try{
			var _tmpProfileCategory = this.getCookie("ioldmpprof");
			//_tmpProfileCategory = _tmpProfileCategory.replace("93078,","");
			return _tmpProfileCategory;
		}catch(ex){
			if(this.debug) {
				console.log(ex);
			}
		}
	},

	biIolPositionMap: function(objBiToTrack){
		try{
			var $this = $(objBiToTrack);
			var _tmpPos = $this.offset();
			return parseInt(_tmpPos.left + 50 * _tmpPos.top);
		}catch(ex){return 0;}
	},


	biIolInitPositionStrilli: function(){
		for (var eI=0;eI<this.config.biA.length;eI++){
			try{
				if (this.config.biA[eI]){
					if(this.config.biA[eI].t){
						if (this.config.biA[eI].t=="iolmpck"){
							var _trCanale = this.biIolTrCanale($(this.config.biA[eI].e).attr('data-bi-canale'), $(this.config.biA[eI].e).attr('data-bi-url'));
							if($(this.config.biA[eI].e).offset()){
								this.positionBox.push( {'id': this.config.biA[eI].e,'position': $(this.config.biA[eI].e).offset().top, 'bi':false, 'idc': this.biIolTrIdDetail(_trCanale, $(this.config.biA[eI].e).attr('data-bi-id')), 'dataBiParam': $(this.config.biA[eI].e).attr('data-bi-param'), 'dataBiId': $(this.config.biA[eI].e).attr('data-bi-id') });
							}
						}
					}
				}
		 	this.timerBI = setInterval("lBI.biIolRilevaDivVisualizzati()",this.biIolDelay);
		   }catch(ex){
				if(this.debug) {
					console.log(ex);
				}
				clearInterval(lBI.timerBI);
		   }
		}
	},

	biIolRilevaDivVisualizzati: function () {
		try{
			try{
				var _posTop = this.posTop();
				var _posBottom = this.posBottom();
			}catch(ex){clearInterval(this.timerBI);}


			try{
				var _HpStrilloId = new Array();
				var _Boxes_id = new Array();
				var _dataBiResolution= this.biGetResolutionIolEvent();
				var _blnNotStop = false;
				if (_dataBiResolution == "0-559"){_dataBiResolution="559";}
			}catch(ex){clearInterval(this.timerBI);}

			try{
				for(var j=0;j<this.positionBox.length;j++)
				{
					if	(this.positionBox[j].bi==false)
						_blnNotStop = true;

					if(this.positionBox[j].position > _posTop && this.positionBox[j].position < _posBottom)
					{

						if	(this.positionBox[j].bi==false){

							_HpElementId = this.positionBox[j].idc;

							this.positionBox[j].bi=true;
							if (_HpElementId.indexOf("undefined")== -1) {
								_HpStrilloId.push(_HpElementId);

								var vDataBiId=this.positionBox[j].dataBiId;
								var vDataBiParam=this.positionBox[j].dataBiParam;

								var vArrDataBiParam = vDataBiParam.split("|");


								try{vBiParamMacroArea= vArrDataBiParam[0];}catch(ex){}
								try{vBiParamArea= vArrDataBiParam[1];}catch(ex){}


								_Boxes_id.push({'area' : vBiParamMacroArea, 'box' : vBiParamArea, 'doc_id' : _HpElementId});
							}
						}
					}

				}
			}catch(ex){clearInterval(lBI.timerBI);}

			try{
				if (_HpStrilloId.length>0){

					IOL.EVNT.evMngr.sendEvents(IOL.EVNT.evMngr.getEventUrls("bxmp", {
	                   "domain" : "wwwtest.virgilio.it",
	                   "pag_id" : "hp",
	                   "doc_id" : "",
	                   "doc_type" : 0,
	                   "ref_host" : IOL.EVNT.evMngr.getHostFromUrl(document.referrer),
	                   "ref_path" : IOL.EVNT.evMngr.getPathFromUrl(document.referrer),
	                   "boxes_ctr_id" : _HpStrilloId,   // array di identificativi identici al valore inserito in "box_ctr_id" nel caso di click (usato per il ctr)
	                   "boxes_id" : _Boxes_id, // array di oggetti che identificano il box a fini statistici (in genere ricalcano i dati del click ma non è detto, tra l’altro sono meno articolati)
	                   "breakpoint" : _dataBiResolution,
	                   "source" : "",
	                   "attrs" : []
	                }), function() {} );


					if(this.debug){
						console.log ("id strilli visualizzati: " +  _HpStrilloId);
					}
				}

				if(!_blnNotStop){
					clearInterval(lBI.timerBI);
				}
			}catch(ex){clearInterval(lBI.timerBI);}

		}catch(ex){clearInterval(lBI.timerBI);}
	},

	pageWidth: function() {return window.innerWidth != null? window.innerWidth: document.documentElement && document.documentElement.clientWidth ? document.documentElement.clientWidth:document.body != null? document.body.clientWidth:null;},
	pageHeight: function () {return window.innerHeight != null? window.innerHeight: document.documentElement && document.documentElement.clientHeight ? document.documentElement.clientHeight:document.body != null? document.body.clientHeight:null;},
	posLeft : function () {return typeof window.pageXOffset != 'undefined' ? window.pageXOffset:document.documentElement && document.documentElement.scrollLeft? document.documentElement.scrollLeft:document.body.scrollLeft? document.body.scrollLeft:0;},
	posTop: function() {return typeof window.pageYOffset != 'undefined' ? window.pageYOffset:document.documentElement && document.documentElement.scrollTop? document.documentElement.scrollTop: document.body.scrollTop?document.body.scrollTop:0;},
	posRight: function () {return this.posLeft()+this.pageWidth();},
	posBottom: function () {return this.posTop()+this.pageHeight();},


  getCookie : function (c_name){if(document.cookie.length>0){c_start=document.cookie.indexOf(c_name+"=");if(c_start!=-1){c_start=c_start+c_name.length+1;c_end=document.cookie.indexOf(";",c_start);if(c_end==-1)c_end=document.cookie.length;return unescape(document.cookie.substring(c_start,c_end));}}return"";}


}

				if (typeof mem_order_domain[hh] !== "undefined") {
	      	var mem_order_value = mem_order_domain[hh];
	      	var myLi = jQuery('li[data-order="' + mem_order_value + '"]');
	      	myLi.addClass("active");
	      }
	      else if ((typeof adv_sito !== "undefined") && (adv_sito == "local")) {
	      		mem_order_value="3";
	      		var myLi = jQuery('li[data-order="' + mem_order_value + '"]');
	      		myLi.addClass("active");
	      }
	      else if (typeof debug_voce_menu !== "undefined") {
	      		mem_order_value=""+debug_voce_menu;
	      		var myLi = jQuery('li[data-order="' + mem_order_value + '"]');
	      		myLi.addClass("active");
	      }
	      else if (hh.indexOf(".myblog.it") !== -1) {
              	var mem_order_value = "23";
                var myLi = jQuery('li[data-order="' + mem_order_value + '"]');
                myLi.addClass("active");
              }
	      else {
	      	jQuery.each(mem_order_domain, function(k, v){
					    if (hh.indexOf(k) !== -1) {
					    		var mem_order_value = v;
	      					var myLi = jQuery('li[data-order="' + mem_order_value + '"]');
	      					myLi.addClass("active");
	      					return false;
					    }
					});
	      }
	      
				window.tlb = new toolbar('tlb-corp');
			}

		function toolbar(id){
			_self = this;
			_self.toolDx = jQuery('#'+id+'').find('#tlb-dx').outerWidth(true);
						
			_self.toolSx = jQuery('#'+id+'').find('#tlb-sx');
			_self.toolAlt = jQuery('#'+id+'').find('#tlb-altro');
			_self.toolSpeciali = jQuery('#'+id+'').find('#tbl-speciali');
			
			_self.toolSx_li_orig = _self.toolSx.find('> ul li');
			_self.toolAlt_li_orig = _self.toolAlt.find('> ul li');
			_self.toolSpeciali_li_orig = _self.toolSpeciali.find('> ul li');
			
			_self.minor = false;
			
			_self.check = false;
			
			var iCanUseOn = !!jQuery.fn.on;
			var timeK;
			
			var toolSx = _self.toolSx.outerWidth(true);
			var wind = jQuery(window).width() - 40;
			
			_self.closePanel = function (e){
		        var o=jQuery("#tlb-corp .open");
		        if(o.length>0) {
		            if(o.find(e.target).length == 0) {
		                if(jQuery(window).width() <= 768) {
	                		jQuery('#tlb-corp .open').toggleClass('static')
	                	}
		                jQuery("#tlb-corp .open").removeClass("open");
		            }
		        }
			}
			_self.mnu = function(elm){
				if (iCanUseOn) {
					jQuery(elm).on('click', function(e){
            	_self.closePanel(e);
            	if(jQuery(window).width() <= 768) {
            		jQuery(this).toggleClass('static')
            	}
            	jQuery(this).toggleClass('open')
					})
				}
				else {
					jQuery(elm).bind('click', function(e){
            	timeK=e.timeStamp;
            	if (jQuery(this).hasClass("open")) {
            		_self.closePanel(e);
            	}
            	else {
              	if(jQuery(window).width() <= 768) {
              		jQuery(this).toggleClass('static')
              	}
              	jQuery(this).toggleClass('open');
              }
					})
				}
			}
			_self.moveItem = function(){
				_self.toolSx.find('> ul li:last').prependTo(_self.toolAlt.find('> ul'));
			}
			_self.restoreItem = function(){
				_self.toolAlt.find('> ul li:first').appendTo(_self.toolSx.find('> ul'));
			}
			_self.groupmenu = function() {
				if(_self.toolSx.find('> ul li').length !== 0){
					do {
					    _self.moveItem();
					    toolSx = _self.toolSx.outerWidth(true);

					}while ((toolSx + _self.toolDx) >= wind)
					_self.check = true
				}
			}
			_self.Ungroupmenu = function() {
				if(_self.toolSx.find('> ul li').length >= 11) {
					_self.check = false;
				}else if(_self.toolAlt.find('ul > li:last').outerWidth(true) <= wind -(_self.toolDx+toolSx)){
					_self.restoreItem();
				}
			}
			
			_self.RestoreUl = function() {
				 _self.toolSx.find('> ul ').html(_self.toolSx_li_orig);
				 _self.toolAlt.find('> ul ').html(_self.toolAlt_li_orig);
				 _self.toolSpeciali.find('> ul ').html(_self.toolSpeciali_li_orig);
			}
			_self.checkWidth = function(){
				if(jQuery(window).width() <= 768) {
					
					_self.minor = true;
					
					//console.log("_self.checkWidth < 768");
					
					var lis0 = _self.toolSx.find('> ul li');
					
					var lis1 = _self.toolAlt.find('> ul li');
					
					var lis2 = _self.toolSpeciali.find('> ul li');
					
					var lis_tmp = lis0.add(lis1);
					
					var lis = lis2.add(lis_tmp);
					//console.log(lis);
					
			    lis = lis.sort(function(a,b){
			       var num1 = parseInt(jQuery(a).attr("data-order"), 10),
			           num2 = parseInt(jQuery(b).attr("data-order"), 10);
			       if (num1 == 'undefined') {num1 = 20;}
			       if (num2 == 'undefined') {num2 = 20;}
			       
			       //console.log(num1, num2);
			       if (num1 > num2) return 1;
			       if (num1 < num2) return -1;
			       return 0;
			    });
			    
			    _self.toolAlt.find('> ul ').empty();
			    
			    _self.toolAlt.find('> ul ').html(lis);
			    
				} else {
					//console.log("_self.checkWidth > 768");
					if (_self.minor) {
						_self.RestoreUl();
					}
					
					_self.minor = false;
					
					if((toolSx + _self.toolDx) >= (wind)){
						_self.groupmenu();
					}else if(((wind) - _self.toolDx) >= toolSx && _self.toolSx.find('> ul li').length <= 10){
						_self.Ungroupmenu();
					}
				}
			}
			if (iCanUseOn) {
				jQuery(window).on('resize',function(){
					 var first_resize_bug = false;
					 
					 jQuery(function() {
	
					    var timer_id;
					
							if (!first_resize_bug) {
								first_resize_bug = true;
								clearTimeout(timer_id);
					
				        timer_id = setTimeout(function() {
				
				            toolSx = _self.toolSx.outerWidth(true);
										_self.toolDx = jQuery('#'+id+'').find('#tlb-dx').outerWidth(true);
										wind = jQuery(window).width() - 40;
										_self.checkWidth();
				
				        }, 200);
				        
							}
							
					    jQuery(window).resize(function() {
					
					        clearTimeout(timer_id);
					
					        timer_id = setTimeout(function() {
					
					            toolSx = _self.toolSx.outerWidth(true);
											_self.toolDx = jQuery('#'+id+'').find('#tlb-dx').outerWidth(true);
											wind = jQuery(window).width() - 40;
											_self.checkWidth();
					
					        }, 200);
					    });
					});
				})
			}
			else {
				jQuery(window).bind('resize',function(){
					 var first_resize_bug = false;
					 
					 jQuery(function() {
	
					    var timer_id;
					
							if (!first_resize_bug) {
								first_resize_bug = true;
								clearTimeout(timer_id);
					
				        timer_id = setTimeout(function() {
				
				            toolSx = _self.toolSx.outerWidth(true);
										_self.toolDx = jQuery('#'+id+'').find('#tlb-dx').outerWidth(true);
										wind = jQuery(window).width() - 40;
										_self.checkWidth();
				
				        }, 200);
				        
							}
							
					    jQuery(window).resize(function() {
					
					        clearTimeout(timer_id);
					
					        timer_id = setTimeout(function() {
					
					            toolSx = _self.toolSx.outerWidth(true);
											_self.toolDx = jQuery('#'+id+'').find('#tlb-dx').outerWidth(true);
											wind = jQuery(window).width() - 40;
											_self.checkWidth();
					
					        }, 200);
					    });
					});
				})
			}
			
			_self.mnu('#tlb-user');
			_self.mnu('#tlb-altro');
			if (iCanUseOn) {
				jQuery("html").on('click', function(e){
	      	_self.closePanel(e)
				});
			}
			else {
				jQuery("html").bind('click', function(e){
	      	if (!jQuery(e.target).closest('#tlb-altro').length && !jQuery(e.target).closest('#tlb-user').length && e.timeStamp !== timeK) {
             _self.closePanel(e);
          }
	      	//_self.closePanel(e)
				});
			}
			
			_self.checkWidth();
		}
</script>

        <script>
      libHP = function() {
  this.debug=false;
  this.currentSlideIdx=0;
  this.currentPageItem=0;
  this.actualPageSlide=0;
  this.totalPage=0;
  this.enterSlideControllerTopNew=false;
  this.enterSlideServizi=false;
  this.enterSlideCibo=false;
  this.enterSlideEsperti=false;
  this.enterSlideVideo=false;
  this.enterSlideCalcio=false;
  this.numItemsperPageController = 5;
  this.firstItemPage=0;
}

libHP.prototype = {
    checkOrientation: function(){
      var currMode = "";

      switch(window.orientation){

           case 0:
           currMode = "portrait";
           break;

           case -90:
           currMode = "landscape";
           break;

           case 90:
           currMode = "landscape";
           break;

           case 180:
           currMode = "landscape";
           break;
     }

     return currMode;
    },

    // dato un elemnto restiruisce se è visible in pagina o meno in quel momento
    isScrolledIntoView: function (elem){
      var $elem = $(elem);
      var $window = $(window);

      var docViewTop = $window.scrollTop();
      var docViewBottom = docViewTop + $window.height();

      var elemTop = $elem.offset().top;
      var elemBottom = elemTop + $elem.height();

      return ((elemTop <= docViewBottom) && (elemTop >= docViewTop));
     // return (elemTop >= docViewTop);
    },

    // Gestisce l'autoplay dello swipper slide a seconda che sia visibile o meno
    slideVisibleStartStop : function (objSlide, strIdElement) {
                            if (objSlide.autoplaying && !libHP.isScrolledIntoView(strIdElement)){
                              objSlide.stopAutoplay();
                              if (this.debug){
                                console.log("slideVisibleStartStop " + strIdElement + " stop");
                              }
                            }
                            else if (!objSlide.autoplaying && libHP.isScrolledIntoView(strIdElement)){
                              objSlide.startAutoplay();
                              if (this.debug){
                                console.log("slideVisibleStartStop " + strIdElement + " start");
                              }
                            }
     },

     // Gestisce il cambio pagina con il controller
     slideChange : function (swiper, swiperController, tmd){
     	     					if(typeof tmd === 'undefined') tmd = 200;
                    this.currentSlideIdx =  swiper.activeIndex % swiper.loopedSlides;

                    this.currentPageItem = Math.floor(this.currentSlideIdx/this.numItemsperPageController);
                    this.firstItemPage = this.currentPageItem * this.numItemsperPageController;


                    if (this.currentPageItem < 0){
                       this.currentPageItem = Math.floor(swiper.loopedSlides/this.numItemsperPageController);
                    }

                    console.log ("this.actualPageSlide " + this.actualPageSlide);
                    console.log ("this.currentPageItem " + this.currentPageItem);

                    //Se l'elemento dello slider grande è nella pagina seguente dello slider controller
                    //allora devo far cambiare pagina allo slider sotto
                    if(this.actualPageSlide < this.currentPageItem){

                       //Setto la pagina attuale dello slider sotto come la pagina dell'elemento corrente.
                       this.actualPageSlide = this.currentPageItem;

                       //allora lo slider controller deve seguire lo slider grande e andare al gruppo successivo
                       //di slide
                       console.log('swiperController.slideNext');
                       swiperController.slideNext(null,tmd);
                    } else if(this.actualPageSlide > this.currentPageItem){

                       //Setto la pagina attuale dello slider sotto come la pagina dell'elemento corrente.
                       this.actualPageSlide = this.currentPageItem;

                       //Oppure al gruppo precedente di slide
                       console.log('swiperController.slidePrev');
                       swiperController.slidePrev(null,tmd);
                    }

                    $('#hp_tn-controller LI').removeClass("swiper-slide-active");
                    $("#hp_tn-controller LI[data-swiper-slide-index='" + this.currentSlideIdx +"']").addClass("swiper-slide-active");

              if (this.debug){
                    console.log('Debugging slides:');
                    console.log ("swiper.loopedSlides " + swiper.loopedSlides);
                    console.log ("this.currentSlideIdx " + this.currentSlideIdx);
                    console.log ("this.currentPageItem " + this.currentPageItem);
                    console.log ("this.firstItemPage " + this.firstItemPage);
                    console.log ("this.actualPageSlide " + this.actualPageSlide);
                    console.log ("this.totalPage " + this.totalPage);
              }

     },

     //Restituisce il numero di pagine su cui fare lo slide
     slidePositionWithPagination : function (objSlide, objSlideTop, numPageToSlide) {

       /* this.currentSlideIdx=  objSlideTop.activeIndex - objSlideTop.loopedSlides;

        if(objSlideTop.activeIndex < (objSlideTop.loopedSlides+1)){
           this.currentSlideIdx=  objSlideTop.activeIndex;

        }*/
        this.currentSlideIdx=  objSlideTop.activeIndex % objSlideTop.loopedSlides;

        this.currentPageItem = Math.floor(this.currentSlideIdx/this.numItemsperPageController );



        this.actualPageSlide = (this.currentPageItem + numPageToSlide);


        this.totalPage =Math.floor(objSlide.loopedSlides/this.numItemsperPageController );


        if (this.actualPageSlide<0){
            if (objSlide.loopedSlides%this.numItemsperPageController >0)
             this.actualPageSlide = this.totalPage;
           else
             this.actualPageSlide = this.totalPage-1;
        }
        else if (this.actualPageSlide>this.totalPage){
          this.actualPageSlide = 0;
        }

        // if (this.debug){
         console.log("SLIDER: actual idx " + this.currentSlideIdx + " - actual page " + this.currentPageItem + " - next " + this.actualPageSlide);
       // }

        // console.log('objSlide.slideTo');
        // objSlide.slideTo((this.actualPageSlide*this.numItemsperPageController ),200);

        var currentSlideId = objSlide.activeIndex - objSlide.loopedSlides;

        if(objSlide.activeIndex < objSlide.loopedSlides){
           currentSlideId = objSlide.activeIndex;
        }

        //E faccio scattare dopo 200ms lo slide dello slider sopra
        setTimeout(function(){console.log('objSlideTop.slideTo setTimeout');objSlideTop.slideTo(currentSlideId,0);},200);

     },

     // Gestisce il cambio pagina con il controller
     slideChangeIE : function (swiper, swiperController){

                    var _loopSlides = $("#hp_tn-container").find(".swiper-slide").not(".swiper-slide-duplicate").length;
                    this.currentSlideIdx =  (swiper.activeIndex-1) % _loopSlides;
                    console.log ("this.currentSlideIdx " + this.currentSlideIdx);


                    this.currentPageItem = Math.floor(this.currentSlideIdx/this.numItemsperPageController);
                    console.log ("this.currentPageItem " + this.currentPageItem);
                    this.firstItemPage = this.currentPageItem * this.numItemsperPageController;
                    console.log ("this.firstItemPage " + this.firstItemPage);


                    if (this.currentPageItem < 0){
                       this.currentPageItem = Math.floor(_loopSlides/this.numItemsperPageController);
                       console.log ("this.firstItemPage " + this.firstItemPage);
                    }


                    if(this.actualPageSlide != this.currentPageItem){
                       this.actualPageSlide = this.currentPageItem;
                       swiperController.swipeTo(this.firstItemPage,200);
                    }
                    else{
                        $('#hp_tn-controller LI').removeClass("swiper-slide-active");
                        $("#hp_tn-controller li:not(.swiper-slide-duplicate):eq(" +  this.currentSlideIdx + ")").addClass("swiper-slide-active");
                    }
              // if (this.debug){
                    console.log ("this.currentSlideIdx " + this.currentSlideIdx);
                    console.log ("this.currentPageItem " + this.currentPageItem);
                    console.log ("this.firstItemPage " + this.firstItemPage);
                    console.log ("this.actualPageSlide " + this.actualPageSlide);
                    console.log ("this.totalPage " + this.totalPage);
              // }

     },
     mouseEnterIE: function(swiper, swiperController){
         var _loopSlides = $("#hp_tnc-container").find(".swiper-slide").not(".swiper-slide-duplicate").length;
         this.currentSlideIdx =  (swiperController.activeIndex - 1) % _loopSlides;

         console.log(swiperController.activeIndex);
        //  this.currentPageItem = Math.floor(this.currentSlideIdx/this.numItemsperPageController);
        //  this.firstItemPage = this.currentPageItem * this.numItemsperPageController;
        //  if (this.currentPageItem < 0){
        //    this.currentPageItem = Math.floor(_loopSlides/this.numItemsperPageController);
        //    console.log ("this.firstItemPage " + this.firstItemPage);
        // }

        swiper.swipeTo(this.currentSlideIdx, 0);

     },

     //Restituisce il numero di pagine su cui fare lo slide for IE
     slidePositionWithPaginationIE : function (objSlide, objSlideTop, numPageToSlide) {

        /*this.currentSlideIdx=  objSlideTop.activeIndex - objSlideTop.loopedSlides;

        if(objSlideTop.activeIndex < (objSlideTop.loopedSlides+1)){
           this.currentSlideIdx=  objSlideTop.activeIndex;

        }*/
        var _loopSlides = $("#hp_tn-container").find(".swiper-slide").not(".swiper-slide-duplicate").length;
        this.currentSlideIdx =   (objSlideTop.activeIndex-1) % _loopSlides;


        this.currentPageItem = Math.floor(this.currentSlideIdx/this.numItemsperPageController );



        this.actualPageSlide = (this.currentPageItem+numPageToSlide);

        var _loopSlides = $("#hp_tn-controller").find(".swiper-slide").not(".swiper-slide-duplicate").length; //objSlide.loopedSlides
        this.totalPage =Math.floor(_loopSlides/this.numItemsperPageController );


        if (this.actualPageSlide<0){
              if (_loopSlides%this.numItemsperPageController >0)
               this.actualPageSlide = this.totalPage;
             else
               this.actualPageSlide = this.totalPage-1;
        }
        else if (this.actualPageSlide>this.totalPage){
          this.actualPageSlide = 0;
        }


        if (this.debug){
         console.log("SLIDER IE: actual idx " + this.currentSlideIdx + " - actual page" + this.currentPageItem + " - next " + this.actualPageSlide);
       }

    var currentSlideId = (this.actualPageSlide*this.numItemsperPageController );



    objSlide.swipeTo(currentSlideId,200);
        objSlideTop.swipeTo(currentSlideId,200);

     },
};

function getMainSizeState() {
    var mainSize,
        hpMainWidth = $('#hp_main').width();

    if(hpMainWidth < 425){
        return mainSize = 1;
    }
    if(hpMainWidth >= 425 && hpMainWidth < 768){
        return mainSize = 2;
    }
    if(hpMainWidth >= 768 && hpMainWidth < 1000){
        return mainSize = 3;
    }
    if(hpMainWidth >= 1000 && hpMainWidth < 1192){
        return mainSize = 4;
    }
    if (hpMainWidth >= 1192) {
        return mainSize = 5;
    }
}

if (!Array.prototype.some) {
  Array.prototype.some = function(fun/*, thisArg*/) {
    'use strict';

    if (this == null) {
      throw new TypeError('Array.prototype.some called on null or undefined');
    }

    if (typeof fun !== 'function') {
      throw new TypeError();
    }

    var t = Object(this);
    var len = t.length >>> 0;

    var thisArg = arguments.length >= 2 ? arguments[1] : void 0;
    for (var i = 0; i < len; i++) {
      if (i in t && fun.call(thisArg, t[i], i, t)) {
        return true;
      }
    }

    return false;
  };
}

        function popUpShare(bt) {
            var tit = bt.parents(".hp_share").attr("data-tit"), url = bt.parents(".hp_share").attr("data-link");
            if (bt.hasClass("hp_share-fb")) {
                shareUrl = "http://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=" + encodeURI(url);
            } else if (bt.hasClass("hp_share-tw")) {
                var rtit = tit;
                rtit = rtit.replace("\\u00e8", "è").replace("\\u00e9", "é").replace("\\u2019", "'").replace("\\u00e0", "à").replace("\\u00ec", "ì").replace("\\u00f2", "ò").replace("\\u00f9", "ù").replace("\\u0022", '"');
                shareUrl = "https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?via=virgilio_it&text=" + encodeURI(rtit) + "&url=" + encodeURI(url);
            } else {
                shareUrl = "https://plus.google.com/share?url=" + encodeURI(url);
            }
            window.open(shareUrl, "shr", "height=400,width=500,toolbar=no,menubar=no,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes,location=no,status=no");
        }
    };
})(jQuery);
//e: share tool

//s: animation roller
(function($) {
    $.fn.animationRoller = function(options) {
        var settings = $.extend({
            speed: 100, //px
            roller: null,
            milliseconds: false,
            animationClass: '',
            onlyIfBigger: false,
            removeWidths: [],
            ieCompatibility: false,
            animationName: '', //needed for ieCompatibility
            animationTimingFunction: 'linear', //optional
            animationIterationCount: 'infinite', //optional
            animationFillMode: 'none', //optional
            animationDirection: 'normal', //optional
            animationDelay: '0s', //optional
        }, options);

        if(!settings.roller){
            return this;
        }


        if(settings.ieCompatibility && !settings.animationName){
            throw new Error('When in IE compatibility mode, you must specify an animation name');
        }

        var el = this.find(settings.roller);
        var container = this;

        if(el.length === 0){
            return this;
        }

        function animate() {
            if(settings.animationClass){
                el.removeClass(settings.animationClass);
            }
            var elWidth = el.width();
            if(settings.animationClass){
                el.addClass(settings.animationClass);
            }
            var containerWidth = container.width();

            $.each(settings.removeWidths, function(index, element) {
                containerWidth -= container.find(element).outerWidth();
            });

            if(settings.onlyIfBigger) {
                if(containerWidth > elWidth){
                    if(settings.animationClass){
                        el.removeClass(settings.animationClass);
                    }
                    return;
                }
            }

            var animationDuration = parseInt((elWidth + containerWidth) / settings.speed);
            animationDuration+= (settings.milliseconds) ? 'ms' : 's';

            if(settings.ieCompatibility && settings.animationName){
                el.css({
                    'animation-name': settings.animationName,
                    'animation-timing-function': settings.animationTimingFunction,
                    'animation-delay': settings.animationDelay,
                    'animation-iteration-count': settings.animationIterationCount,
                    'animation-fill-mode': settings.animationFillMode,
                    'animation-direction': settings.animationDirection,
                    'animation-duration': animationDuration,
                });
            } else {
                el.css({
                    '-webkit-animation-duration': animationDuration,
                    'animation-duration': animationDuration
                });
            }

            if(settings.animationClass) {
                el.addClass(settings.animationClass);
            }
        }

        animate();

        $(window).on('resize', function() {
            animate();
        });

        return this;
    };
})(jQuery);

$('.hp_flash-news').animationRoller({
    speed: 90,
    roller: '.hp_news > span',
    onlyIfBigger: true,
    animationClass: 'hp_roller-txt',
    removeWidths: [
        '.hp_tit',
    ],
    ieCompatibility: true,
    animationName: 'roller',
});

(function($) {
    $.fn.dynamicMenu = function(options) {

        if(isIe8){
            return this;
        }

        var settings = $.extend({
            entryEl: '.hp_menu-el',
            onResize: true,
        }, options);

        var $moreMenu = $('<nav class="hp_dropdown">' +
                            '<div>ALTRO</div>' +
                            '<ul class="hp_menu-list-more">' +
                            '</ul>' +
                        '</nav>');

        // var $elOutOfRangeTemplate = $('<li class="hp_menu-el hp_menu-out-of-range"><a href="#" target="_blank"></a></li>');

        if(this.length === 0 || this.length > 1) {
            return this;
        }

        var dynamicMenu = this;
        var $entries = dynamicMenu.find(settings.entryEl);

        var calcMaxWidth = function() {
            return dynamicMenu.width();
        };

        var entriesWidths = $entries.get().map(function(a) {
            return $(a).outerWidth(true);
        });

        var calcEntriesWidth = function() {
            return dynamicMenu.find(settings.entryEl).get().reduce(function(a, b) {
                return a + $(b).outerWidth();
            }, 0);
        };

        var calcDropdownWidth = function() {
            return 44 + 11; //Larghezza del bottone altro + larghezza della freccina
        };

        var checkFit = function(){
            return calcMaxWidth() > calcEntriesWidth() + calcDropdownWidth();
        };

        var appendDropdown = function() {
            dynamicMenu.append($moreMenu);
        };

        var appendLastToDropdown = function(){
            dynamicMenu.find(settings.entryEl).not('.hp_menu-out-of-range').last().addClass('hp_menu-out-of-range').prependTo($moreMenu.find('ul'));
        };

        var isLastInDropdown = function() {
            return $moreMenu.find('.hp_menu-out-of-range').length === 1;
        };

        var isDropdownEmpty = function() {
            return $moreMenu.find('.hp_menu-out-of-range').length === 0;
        };

        var canExpandMenu = function() {
            var firstToPutBack = dynamicMenu.find(settings.entryEl).not('.hp_menu-out-of-range').length;
            if(isLastInDropdown()){
                return calcMaxWidth() > calcEntriesWidth() - calcDropdownWidth() + entriesWidths[firstToPutBack];
            } else {
                return calcMaxWidth() > calcEntriesWidth() + calcDropdownWidth() +  entriesWidths[firstToPutBack];
            }
        };

        var appendFromDropdownToMenu = function() {
            $moreMenu.find('.hp_menu-out-of-range').first().removeClass('hp_menu-out-of-range').appendTo(dynamicMenu.find('.hp_menu-list'));
        };

        var removeDropdown = function() {
            $moreMenu.remove();
        };

        var execute = function() {
            if (getMainSizeState() < 5) {
                if(checkFit()) {
                    var i = 0;
                    while (canExpandMenu() === true && i < 20) {
                        appendFromDropdownToMenu();
                        i++;
                    }
                    if(isDropdownEmpty()) {
                        removeDropdown();
                    }
                } else {
                    var j = 0;
                    while(checkFit() === false && j < 20) {
                        appendLastToDropdown();
                        j++;
                    }
                    appendDropdown();
                }
            } else {
                var i = 0;
                while (canExpandMenu() === true && i < 20) {
                    appendFromDropdownToMenu();
                    i++;
                }
                if(isDropdownEmpty()) {
                    removeDropdown();
                }
            }
        };

        execute();

        if(settings.onResize) {
            $(window).resize(function(){
                execute();
            });
        }

        return this;
    };
})(jQuery);

$('#hp_main-menu').dynamicMenu();

	});
}

var loadContent20Pics = (function () {
	/* load content20 images only if needed */
	var res=getMainSizeState();
	var content20Load=function(){
		if(res<5){
			var m=document.getElementById('hp_main');
			var list = m.getElementsByTagName("IMG");
			for(var i=0;i<list.length;i++){
				var u=list[i].getAttribute('data-lsrc');
				if(u){
					list[i].src=u;
					list[i].removeAttribute('data-lsrc');
				}
			}
		}
	}
	content20Load();
	$(window).on({
  	'resize orientationchange': function() {
  		var r=getMainSizeState();
  		if(res!=r){
				res=r;
				setTimeout(function(){content20Load();console.log('ll');},300);
			}
		}
	});

})();

var fixUnfixHeader = (function () {
	/* show/hide superheader & */
	/* load images after first scroll */
	var stat = false;
	var bod=$('body');
	var mai=$('#hp_main');
    var header = $('#hp_header').length > 0;
	var res=getMainSizeState();
	if(typeof _brandheader == 'undefined') _brandheader=false;
	var lazy=false;
	var rawLazy=function(){
		var m=document.getElementById('hp_main');
		var list = m.getElementsByTagName("IMG");
		for(var i=0;i<list.length;i++){
			var u=list[i].getAttribute('data-rsrc');
			if(u){
				list[i].src=u;
				list[i].removeAttribute('data-rsrc');
			}
		}
	}
	var manageFixed=function(){
		var scrll = $(window).scrollTop();
		var off_set = mai.offset().top;
	  if ((scrll >= off_set)&&(stat==false)){
        if(header){
    	  	if(_brandheader)bod.addClass("header_fixed").removeClass("header_anim").removeClass("header_brand");
    		else bod.addClass("header_fixed").removeClass("header_anim");
    	  	setTimeout(function(){$('body').addClass('header_anim')},10);
    	  	stat=true;
        }
	  	if(!lazy){
	  		lazy=true;
	  		setTimeout(function(){rawLazy()},100);
	  	}
	  }else if((scrll < off_set)&&(stat==true)){
        if(header){
    	  	bod.removeClass('header_fixed');
    		if(_brandheader)bod.removeClass('header_fixed').addClass('header_brand');
    		else bod.removeClass('header_fixed');
    	  	stat=false;
        }
	  }
	};
	manageFixed();

	$(window).on({
  	'resize orientationchange': function() {
  		var r=getMainSizeState();
  		if(res!=r){
				setTimeout(function(){rawLazy();console.log('rl');},200);
				res=r;
			}
		}
	});

	$(window).scroll(manageFixed);
})();

(function($) {
    $.fn.localPrompt = function( options ) {

        var el = this;
        var boxLocalChoice   = el.find('.hp_local-choice'),
            boxInputCitta    = boxLocalChoice.find('.hp_local-inputs'),
            boxSuggestion    = boxLocalChoice.find('.hp_local-suggestions'),
            boxHistory       = boxLocalChoice.find('.hp_local-last'),
            submitButton     = boxLocalChoice.find('input[type=submit]');

        el.idx = 0;

        var cambiaCittaCallback = function(comuni){
            var suggHTML = '';

            boxHistory.hide();
            if (comuni.length > 0) {
                var limit =  Math.min(5, comuni.length);
                suggHTML += '<h5 class="hp_tit">Scegli una località dalla lista:</h5>' + '<ul>';
                for (var i = 0; i < limit; i++) {
                    suggHTML += '<li class="hp_local-comune-sel" data-nome="' + comuni[i] + '">' + comuni[i] + '</li>\r\n';
                }
                suggHTML += '</ul>';
            } else {
                suggHTML += '<div class="hp_local-comune-error">Specifica una località</div>';
            }
            boxSuggestion.html(suggHTML);
        };

        //s: local choice callbacks
        function localSetCookie(){
            console.log('localSetCookie');
            var n = $(settings.input).val().replace(/\([a-zA-Z]*\)/g, '').trim();
            var t = new Date().getTime();
            var u = 'http://italia.virgilio.it/helper/setistat.php?nome=' + n + '&callBackUrl=1&t=' + t;
            $('<iframe />', {
                name: 'vlocal_setcookie_iframe',
                id: 'vlocal_setcookie_iframe',
                src: u
            }).appendTo('body');
        }

        function fill(h) {
            el.find(settings.input).val(h);
        }

        var settings = $.extend({
            // These are the defaults.
            url: "", // Url delle API da cui prendere la lista dei suggerimenti
            closeButton: ".hp_bt-close", //Classe o ID del bottone che chiude il popup
            toggleButton: ".hp_local-change", //Classe o ID del bottone che apre il popup
            preventDefault: true,
            jsonpCallback: cambiaCittaCallback,
            input: ''
        }, options);

        var delayInput = (function(){
            var timer = 0;
            return function(callback, ms){
                clearTimeout (timer);
                timer = setTimeout(callback, ms);
            };
        })();

        // Show prompt
        el.on('click', settings.toggleButton, function(e){
            if(settings.preventDefault){
                e.preventDefault();
            }
            el.toggleClass('hp_open');
        });

        // Searching when writing
        el.on('keyup', settings.input, function(e){
            console.log('keyup', e);
            var $self = $(this);
            if($self.val() == '') {
                boxSuggestion.html('');
                boxHistory.show();
                return;
            }

            //Pick the suggestions
            var choices = el.find('.hp_local-suggestions .hp_local-comune-sel');

            var keyCode = e.which || e.keyCode;
            switch (keyCode) {
                //If a person press the enter key
                case 13:
                    //Do not submit the form
                    e.preventDefault();

                    //If the suggestion list is present and there is only one suggestion...
                    if(choices.length === 1) {

                        //track user behavior ONLY with fake click
                        submitButton.trigger('click');

                        //... use it that as chosen city
                        choices.click();
                    } else if(choices.length > 1) {

                        //Save jQuery objects for later
                        var $choices = choices;

                        //Get the array of suggestion values...
                        choices  = choices.map(function(){

                            //...without city code, cleaned up a bit
                            return $(this).data('nome').replace(/\([a-zA-Z]*\)/g, '').trim().toLowerCase();
                        }).get();

                        //And check if it matches exactly with what the user wrote
                        var val = $(this).val().replace(/\([a-zA-Z]*\)/g, '').trim().toLowerCase();
                        var eqEl = choices.indexOf(val);

                        //If there's a match
                        if(eqEl > -1) {

                            //track user behavior ONLY with fake click
                            submitButton.trigger('click');

                            //and click on that choice
                            $choices.eq(eqEl).click();
                        } else {
                            //Show "choose from the list below"
                            var errorMessage = el.find('.hp_local-suggestions .hp_tit');
                            errorMessage.removeClass('hp_glow').show();
                            // errorMessage[0].offsetWidth = errorMessage[0].offsetWidth; //trick to reset animation
                            // errorMessage.addClass('hp_glow');
                        }
                    }
                    return false;
                //Arrow down
                case 40:
                    if(choices.length > 0){
                        if(el.idx < choices.length){
                            el.idx++;
                            var liSelected = choices.eq(el.idx - 1);
                            fill(liSelected.text());
                        }
                    }
                    return false;
                //Arrow up
                case 38:
                    if (el.idx < 2) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        return false;
                    } else {
                        el.idx--;
                        var liSelected = choices.eq(el.idx - 1);
                        fill(liSelected.text());
                    }
                    return false;
                // break;
                default:
                    el.idx = 0;
                break;
            }


            delayInput(function(){
                $.ajax({
                    url: settings.url,
                    dataType: "jsonp",
                    jsonp: 'jsonpCallback',
                    data: {
                        dove: $(e.target).val(),
                    },
                    success: settings.jsonpCallback,
                });
            },
            400);
        });

        el.on('keydown', settings.input, function(e){
            var keyCode = e.which || e.keyCode;
            if(keyCode === 13) {
                e.preventDefault();
                return false;
            }
        });

        // Hide prompt
        $(settings.closeButton).on('click', function(){
            el.removeClass('hp_open');
        });

        el.on('click', '.hp_local-comune-sel', function(){

            //Fallback if some JS error or CORS exception happen
            setTimeout(function(){
                window.location.reload();
            }, 3000);
            fill($(this).html());
            localSetCookie();
        });

        //Only on suggestions, NOT on history
        el.on('click', '.hp_local-suggestions .hp_local-comune-sel', function(){

            //track user behavior with fake click
            submitButton.trigger('click');
        });

        submitButton.on('click', function(e){
            e.preventDefault();
            console.log('Submit prevented!');

            //Only if is real click
            if(!e.isTrigger){ //(e.originalEvent !== undefined) as an alternative
                //triggering an ENTER event
                var toBeTriggeredEvent = jQuery.Event('keyup', {which: 13});
                $(settings.input).trigger(toBeTriggeredEvent);
            }
        });

        return this;
    };
}(jQuery));


/* suggerimenti */


function addEvent(obj, evType, fn){
	    if (obj.addEventListener) {
	        obj.addEventListener(evType, fn, false);
	        return true;
	    } else if (obj.attachEvent) {
	        var r = obj.attachEvent("on" + evType, fn);
	        return r;
	    }
}

function Vescape(str){
	var ar1=["%F2","%E0","%F9","%E8","%E9","%EC"];
	var ar2=["%C3%B2","%C3%A0","%C3%B9","%C3%A8","%C3%A9","%C3%AC"];
	var s=escape(str);
	for(var i=0;i<ar1.length;i++){
		s=s.replace(ar1[i],ar2[i]);
	}
	return s;
}

var as={
	'mngSucc': function(o){
		var h='',r=[], tr=sugg01.curStr.toLowerCase(),nsug=0;
		if(o)
			if((o.results)||(o.resultsfuzzy)) {
				if(o.results)if(o.results.length>0){
					h='<ul>';
					for(var i=0;i<10;i++){
						if(i<o.results.length){
							h=h+'<li>';
							var v=o.results[i].value;
							h=h+v;
							h=h+'</li>';
							r[i]=v.replace(/<\/?[^>]+(>|$)/g, "");
							nsug++;
						}
					}
				}
				if(o.resultsfuzzy) if(o.resultsfuzzy.length>0){
					if(h=='')h='<ul>';
					for(var i=0;i<10-nsug;i++){
						if(i<o.resultsfuzzy.length){
							h=h+'<li>';
							var v=o.resultsfuzzy[i].value;
							h=h+v;
							h=h+'</li>';
							r[i]=v.replace(/<\/?[^>]+(>|$)/g, "");
						}
					}
				}
				if (h!='')h=h+'</ul>';
		sugg01.callback(h,r);
	}
}

function HYP_SUGG(myconf){
	var that=this;
	var conf={
		'input': 'q',
		'sugg': 'sugg',
		'request': '',
		'submit_fx': function(){},
		'minlen':2,
		'mouseover':true,
		'input2':false,
		'requesttime':200,
		'charset':''
	};
	if(typeof(myconf)!='undefined')for(var attr in myconf){conf[attr]=myconf[attr]}
	var inputOb,inputOb2,suggOb,suggCl='',stat=0,stuff=[],lis=[],tmr=-1,blockd=0,prev=0,etmr=-1;
	this.block=0;
	this.curStr='';
	this.sel=-1;
	var setup=function(){
		inputOb=document.getElementById(conf.input);
		suggOb=document.getElementById(conf.sugg);
		suggCl=suggOb.className;
		addEvent(inputOb, 'keyup', function(e){e=(e)?e:((window.event)?event:null);return(key(e,0))});
		addEvent(inputOb, 'keydown', function(e){e=(e)?e:((window.event)?event:null);return(key(e,1))});
		if(conf.input2){
			inputOb2=document.getElementById(conf.input2);
			addEvent(inputOb2, 'keyup', function(e){e=(e)?e:((window.event)?event:null);return(key(e,0,1))});
			addEvent(inputOb2, 'keydown', function(e){e=(e)?e:((window.event)?event:null);return(key(e,1,1))});
		}
	}
	var request=function(){;
			if(blockd==1){
				prev=1;
				return;
			}
			if(etmr!=-1)clearTimeout(etmr);
			etmr=setTimeout(function(){unblock()},3000);
			blockd=1;
			prev=0;
			var ur=conf.request,tm = new Date().getTime();
			ur=ur.replace(new RegExp("%Q%","g"),Vescape(that.curStr));
			ur=ur.replace(new RegExp("%T%","g"),tm);
			var i2 = document.getElementById('dynajs_'+conf.sugg);
			if (i2) i2.parentNode.removeChild(i2);
			var iddo = document.body;
		  var element = document.createElement('script');
			element.setAttribute('type','text/javascript');
			element.setAttribute('src',ur);
			element.setAttribute('id','dynajs_'+conf.sugg);
			if(conf.charset!=''){
				element.setAttribute('charset',conf.charset);
			}
			iddo.appendChild(element);
	}
	var unblock=function(){
		blockd=0;
		if(etmr!=-1)clearTimeout(etmr);
		etmr=-1;
		setTimeout(function(){request()},1);
	}
	var key=function(evt,ud,org){
		if(that.block==1)return;
		if(typeof(org)=='undefined')org=0;
		if(typeof(ud)=='undefined')ud=0;
		var kc=evt.keyCode;
		var o=this;if(evt.srcElement)o=evt.srcElement;
		if(stat!=0){
			if(ud==1){
				if(kc==27){
					closeMe();
					return;
				}else if((kc==38)&&(parseInt(that.sel)>0)){
					selMe(parseInt(that.sel)-1);
					that.curStr=inputOb.value=stuff[that.sel];
					if(conf.input2)inputOb2.value=stuff[that.sel];
					if(evt.preventDefault)evt.preventDefault();
					return false;
				} else if((kc==40)&&(parseInt(that.sel)<(lis.length-1))){
					selMe(parseInt(that.sel)+1);
					that.curStr=inputOb.value=stuff[that.sel];
					if(conf.input2)inputOb2.value=stuff[that.sel];
					return false;
				}
				if((kc==27)||(kc==38)||(kc==40))if(evt.preventDefault)evt.preventDefault();
			}
		}

		var s=inputOb.value;
		if(conf.input2){
			if(org==1){
				s=inputOb2.value;
				inputOb.value=s;
			}else{
				inputOb2.value=s;
			}
		}
		if(s)s=that.trim(s);
		if(s!=that.curStr){
			if(tmr!=-1)clearTimeout(tmr);
			tmr=-1;
			that.curStr=s;
			if((s.length<conf.minlen)&&(stat!=0))closeMe();
			else {
				if(s.length>=conf.minlen){
					tmr=setTimeout(function(){request()},conf.requesttime);
				}
			}
		}
		return true;
	}
	var closeMe=function(){
		var c=suggOb.className.replace(" opened","");
		suggOb.className=c;
		suggOb.innerHTML='';
		stuff=[];
		lis=[];
		stat=0;
		this.sel=-1;
	}
	var openMe=function(){
		var c=suggOb.className.replace(" opened","");
		suggOb.className=c+" opened";
		stat=1;
	}
	this.inject=function(htm){
			suggOb.innerHTML=htm;
			openMe();
	}
	this.callback=function(htm,res){
		if(etmr!=-1)clearTimeout(etmr);
		etmr=-1;
		suggOb.innerHTML=htm;
		stuff=res;
		that.sel=-1;
		prepare();
		if(stat==0)openMe();
		blockd=0;
		if(prev==1)setTimeout(function(){request()},1);
	}
	this.selected=function(){
		if(this.sel>-1){
			return(stuff[this.sel]);
		} else if(stuff.length==1){
			inputOb.value=stuff[0];
			if(conf.input2)inputOb2.value=stuff[0];
			return(stuff[0]);
		}		else if(stuff.length>0){
			var mtch=that.curStr.toLowerCase();
			for(var i=0;i<stuff.length;i++){
				var l=stuff[i];
				l=l.toLowerCase();
				var pl=l.indexOf(" (");
				l=l.substring(0,pl);
				if(l==mtch){
					inputOb.value=stuff[i];
					if(conf.input2)inputOb2.value=stuff[i];
					return(stuff[i]);
				}
			}
		}

		/*
		 else if(stuff.length>0){
			var mtch=that.curStr.toLowerCase();
			for(var i=0;i<stuff.length;i++){
				var l=stuff[i];
				l=l.toLowerCase();
				if(l==mtch){
					inputOb.value=stuff[i];
					if(conf.input2)inputOb2.value=stuff[i];
					return(stuff[i]);
				}
			}
		}
		*/
		return(false);
	}
	this.shut=function(blk){
		if(typeof(blk)=='undefined')blk=0;
		that.block=blk;
		if(blk==1){
			inputOb.blur();
			if(conf.input2)inputOb2.blur();
		}
		closeMe();
	}
	var prepare=function(){
		var hc=suggOb.getElementsByTagName("li");
		lis=[];
		var cnt=0;
		for(var i=0;i<hc.length;i++){
			var cls=hc[i].className;
			var ok=0;
			if(!cls)ok=1;
			else if(cls!='error')ok=1;
			if(ok==1){
				addEvent(hc[i], 'mouseover', function(e){e=e||window.event;var o=this;if(e.srcElement)o=e.srcElement;mover(o);return true;});
				addEvent(hc[i], 'mouseout', function(e){e=e||window.event;var o=this;if(e.srcElement)o=e.srcElement;mout(o);return true;});
				addEvent(hc[i], 'click', function(e){e=e||window.event;var o=this;if(e.srcElement)o=e.srcElement;mclick(o);return true;});
				hc[i].setAttribute('data-id',cnt);
				lis[cnt]=hc[i];cnt++;
				hc[i].className='';
			}
		}
	}
	var selMe=function(n){
		if(that.sel!=n)if(parseInt(that.sel)>=0)lis[that.sel].className='';
		if(n<0) {
			that.sel=-1;
		} else {
			that.sel=n;
			lis[that.sel].className='focused';
		}
	}
	var mover=function(o){
		if(that.block==1)return false;
		if(!conf.mouseover)return false;
		var i=o.getAttribute('data-id');
		if(!i) o=o.parentNode;
		i=o.getAttribute('data-id');
		if(!i) o=o.parentNode;
		i=o.getAttribute('data-id');
		if(!i) o=o.parentNode;
		selMe(i);
		if(conf.mouseover) inputOb.value=stuff[i];
		return false;
	}
	var mout=function(o){
		if(that.block==1)return false;
		if(!conf.mouseover)return false;
		var i=o.getAttribute('data-id');
		if(!i) o=o.parentNode;
		i=o.getAttribute('data-id');
		if(!i) o=o.parentNode;
		i=o.getAttribute('data-id');
		if(!i) o=o.parentNode;
		selMe(-1);
		return false;
	}
	var mclick=function(o){
		if(that.block==1)return false;
		var i=o.getAttribute('data-id');
		if(!i) o=o.parentNode;
		i=o.getAttribute('data-id');
		if(!i) o=o.parentNode;
		i=o.getAttribute('data-id');
		if(!i) o=o.parentNode;
		if(that.sel!=-1)if(that.sel!=i)lis[that.sel].className='';
		o.className='focused';
		that.sel=i;
		inputOb.value=stuff[i];
		if(conf.input2)inputOb2.value=stuff[i];
		//conf.submit_fx();

        //track user behavior with fake click
        $('#search input[type=submit]').trigger('click');

		return false;
	}
	this.trim=function(x){
		return x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/gm,'');
	}
	var getPos=function(el){
		for (var lx=0, ly=0;
	  	el != null;
	  	lx += el.offsetLeft, ly += el.offsetTop, el = el.offsetParent);
		return {x: lx,y: ly};
	}
	setup();
}

}

		/* gestione id_strillo */
		var queStri = function () {
		  var query_string = {};
		  var query = window.location.search.substring(1);
		  var vars = query.split("&");
		  for (var i=0;i<vars.length;i++) {
		    var pair = vars[i].split("=");
		        // If first entry with this name
		    if (typeof query_string[pair[0]] === "undefined") {
		      query_string[pair[0]] = decodeURIComponent(pair[1]);
		        // If second entry with this name
		    } else if (typeof query_string[pair[0]] === "string") {
		      var arr = [ query_string[pair[0]],decodeURIComponent(pair[1]) ];
		      query_string[pair[0]] = arr;
		        // If third or later entry with this name
		    } else {
		      query_string[pair[0]].push(decodeURIComponent(pair[1]));
		    }
		  } 
		  return query_string;
		}();

		var initial_slide = 0;

		if(typeof queStri['id_strillo']!='undefined'){
			var ids = queStri['id_strillo'];
			var cnt = 0;
			$("#hp_tn-view li a").each(function(idx){
				if ($(this).attr('data-bi-id') === ids) {
					initial_slide = Math.floor(cnt/2);
				}
				cnt++;
			});
		}

        onSlideChangeEnd: function(swiper) {
            try {
                var currentSlideIdx = swiper.activeIndex - swiper.loopedSlides;
                var currentSlideId = "topslider_" + (currentSlideIdx) + "_link";
                if (swiper.activeIndex < swiper.loopedSlides) {
                    currentSlideIdx = swiper.activeIndex;
                    currentSlideId = "topslider_" + (currentSlideIdx) + "_link";
                }
                //real time tr
                if (!$("#" + currentSlideId).attr('data-bi-viewed')) {
                    lBI.biIolTrView(currentSlideId);
                    $("#" + currentSlideId).attr('data-bi-viewed', true);
                }
            } catch (ex) {
                _initTrElement = currentSlideId;
                $("#" + currentSlideId).attr('data-bi-viewed', true);
            }

            // try {
            //     $('.swiper-slide-prev').find('.hp_tn-pic').addClass('hp_pic-prev');
            // } catch(ex) {

            // }
        },

                console.log(ex);

          function(){
              var url = '/resources/inc/box_live-sport_slide.php?rnd=' + Math.floor((Math.random() * 10000000000) + 1);
              $.ajax({
                  url: url,
                  dataType: 'html',
                  success: function(data){
                        if(data){
                            if($(data).find('.swiper-slide').length > 1){
                                $('.hp_live-sport').removeClass('hp_live-sport-single');
                                if($('.hp_live-sport').find('.swiper-slide').length > 1){
                                    sliderLiveSport.removeAllSlides();
                                    sliderLiveSport.appendSlide($(data).find('.swiper-slide'));
                                } else if($('.hp_live-sport').find('.swiper-slide').length > 0) {
                                    $('.hp_live-sport').find('.swiper-slide').remove();
                                    $(data).find('.swiper-slide').appendTo('.hp_live-sport-view');
                                    sliderLiveSport = new Swiper('.hp_live-sport-container', {
                                        nextButton: '.hp_live-sport-next',
                                        prevButton: '.hp_live-sport-prev',
                                        loop: true,
                                        spaceBetween: 0,

                                        slidesPerGroup: 1,
                                        simulateTouch: false,
                                        speed: 600,
                                        breakpoints: {
                                            767: {
                                                speed: 440
                                            }
                                        }
                                    });
                                }
                                $('.hp_live-sport').find('.swiper-slide').height(sliderLiveSport.height);
                            } else if($(data).find('.swiper-slide').length === 1){
                                $('.hp_live-sport').addClass('hp_live-sport-single');
                                if($('.hp_live-sport').find('.swiper-slide').length > 1){
                                    sliderLiveSport.destroy(false, true);
                                    $('.hp_live-sport').find('.swiper-slide').height(sliderLiveSport.height);
                                }
                                $('.hp_live-sport').find('.swiper-slide').remove();
                                $(data).find('.swiper-slide').appendTo('.hp_live-sport-view');
                            } else {
                                $('.hp_live-sport').remove();
                            }
                        } else {
                            $('.hp_live-sport').remove();
                        }
                    }
              });

    function addSlideTrending(){
        $('.hp_trending')

        sliderTrending = new Swiper('.hp_slide-trending-container', {
            pagination: '.hp_slide-trending-pagination',
            paginationClickable: true,
            loop: true,
            // autoplay: 5000,
            slidesPerView: 2,
            slidesPerGroup: 2,

    function addSlidePiu(){
        $('.hp_box-piu')
        .addClass('hp_piu-slide-container')

        .end()

        sliderPiu = new Swiper('.hp_piu-slide-container', {
            pagination: '.hp_piu-slide-pagination',
            paginationClickable: true,
            loop: true,
            spaceBetween: 0,
            autoplay: 5000,
            slidesPerView: 1,
            slidesPerGroup: 1,
            simulateTouch: false,
            roundLengths: true,
            speed: 600,
            breakpoints: {

                    spaceBetween: 10,
                    speed: 440
                }
            },
		        onInit: function(swiper) {
		            if(autoPlayWatchdog) swiper.stopAutoplay();
		        }
        });

        return slidePiuAdded = true;
    }

        slideBT1Local.addSlider();
        slideBT1Community1.addSlider();
        slideBT1Community2.addSlider();
        slideBT1Food.addSlider();
        slideBT1Extra.addSlider();
        slideBT1Magazine.addSlider();
    }

    // al resize della finestra
    $(window).on({
        'resize orientationchange': function() {
            if(getMainSizeState() <= 2) {
                slideBT1Local.addSlider();
                slideBT1Community1.addSlider();
                slideBT1Community2.addSlider();
                slideBT1Food.addSlider();
                slideBT1Extra.addSlider();
                slideBT1Magazine.addSlider();
            } else if(getMainSizeState() > 2) {
                slideBT1Local.removeSlider();
                slideBT1Community1.removeSlider();
                slideBT1Community2.removeSlider();
                slideBT1Food.removeSlider();
                slideBT1Extra.removeSlider();
                slideBT1Magazine.addSlider();
            }
        }
    });
    //e: script per gestione della slide nel box blockType1

});

//s: SliderManagerBT1 aggiunge classi e div, lancia lo script per lo slider blockType1
function SliderManagerBT1(blockSection){
    return {
        slideBT1Added: false,
        htmlBT1 :  $('.hp_block-' + blockSection + '').html(),
        addSlider: function() {
            if(this.slideBT1Added){
                return;
            }

            $('.hp_block-' + blockSection + '')
            .find('> ul')
                .addClass('hp_block-' + blockSection + '-slide-wrapper swiper-wrapper')
                .wrap('<div class="hp_block-slide-container"></div>')
            .end()
            .find('.hp_story-type2')
                .addClass('swiper-slide')
            .end()
            .append('<div class="hp_block-slide-pagination"></div>');

            this.sliderBlockType1 = new Swiper('.hp_block-' + blockSection + '> .hp_block-slide-container', {
                pagination: '.hp_block-' + blockSection + '> .hp_block-slide-pagination',
                paginationClickable: true,
                loop: true,
                spaceBetween: 10,
                autoplay: 5000,
                slidesPerView: 1,
                slidesPerGroup: 1,
                simulateTouch: false,
                speed: 600,
                breakpoints: {
                    767: {
                        speed: 440
                    }
                },
               	onInit: function(swiper) {
		            	if(autoPlayWatchdog) swiper.stopAutoplay();
		        		}
            });

            this.slideBT1Added = true;

        },
        removeSlider: function() {
            if(!this.slideBT1Added){
                return;
            }

            $('.hp_block-' + blockSection + '')
            .html(this.htmlBT1)
            .find('.hp_share')
                .shareTool();

            this.sliderBlockType1.detachEvents();
            this.slideBT1Added = false;
        }
    }
}
//e: SliderManagerBT1

/* slider title chopper */
function theChopper(div,tag,hx){
	var that=this;
	var ob=document.getElementById(div),titz=[],chopping=0;
	var init = function(){
				var lks = ob.getElementsByTagName(tag);
				var nimg=0;
				for(var i=0;i<lks.length;i++){
					titz[nimg]=lks[i];
					nimg++;
				}
				tryToChop();
				$( window ).load(function() {setTimeout(function(){if(chopping==0)tryToChop()},1)});
	}
	var tryToChop=function(){
		chopping=1;
		var did=0;
		for(var i=0;i<titz.length;i++){
			var h=titz[i].offsetHeight;
			if(h>hx) {
				did=1;
				x=1;
				var d=titz[i].innerHTML;
				var d1=d.lastIndexOf(' ');
				if (d1<1)d1=1;
				var lc=d.substring(d1-1,d1);
				while((lc=='.')||(lc==',')||(lc==';')||(lc==':')||(lc=='-')||(lc=='(')){d1--;lc=d.substring(d1-1,d1)}
				if((lc=='!')||(lc=='?'))d=d.substring(0,d1);
				else d=d.substring(0,d1)+"...";
				titz[i].innerHTML=d;
			}
		}
		if(did==1)setTimeout(tryToChop,20);
		else chopping=0;
	}
	init();
}
/* /slider title chopper */


if(autoPlayWatchdog) setTimeout(autoPlayWatchdogFx, 500);
            </script>
